        function cdnfallback() {
            if (window.appInsights) {
                var region = "UK South";
                var siteName = "acom-prod-uksouth-02";
                var error = new Error('Bundle - client side cdn fallback to local cdn, region: ' + region + ' , sitename: ' + siteName);

                window.appInsights.trackException({ exception: error });
            }

            if (window.location.search.indexOf('cdn=disable') === -1) {
                window.location.href = '?cdn=disable';
            }
        }

  <link rel="dns-prefetch" href="//login.microsoftonline.com" crossorigin> 
  <script>

    $(window).on('load', function () {
        function enableSSO() {
            setTimeout(function () {
                window.addEventListener("message", receiveMessage, false);
                var iframe = document.createElement('iframe');
                iframe.src = '/auth/sso/';
                iframe.setAttribute('id', 'sso-frame');
                iframe.setAttribute('style', 'width: 0; height: 0; border: 0; border: none; position: absolute;');
                iframe.setAttribute('aria-hidden', true);
                $('body').prepend(iframe);
            }, 500);
        }

        function receiveMessage(event) {
            if (event.origin !== 'https://azure.microsoft.com' || event.data !== 'sso-success') {
            return;
            }

            
            window.setTimeout(function () { document.getElementById('sso-frame').contentWindow.location.replace('/auth/sso/'); }, 30 * 60 * 1000);

            
            var enabledSubmitInputs = $('input:enabled[type="submit"], button:enabled[type="submit"]');
            enabledSubmitInputs.attr('disabled', true);

            window.dispatchEvent(createNewEvent('sso.success')); 

            
            $.ajax({ url: '/auth/sso/info/', timeout: 3000 })
                .done(function (data) {
                    if (data) {
                        $('.auth-container').html(data);
                    }
                })
                .fail(function () {
                    
                    enabledSubmitInputs.attr('disabled', false);
                });

            
            $.ajax({ url: '/auth/antiforgerytoken/', timeout: 3000 })
                .done(function (data) {
                    $('input[name="__RequestVerificationToken"]').replaceWith(data);
                    window.dispatchEvent(createNewEvent('sso.requestVerificationTokenReceived'));
                })
                .always(function () {
                    
                    enabledSubmitInputs.attr('disabled', false);
                });
        }

        
        function createNewEvent(eventName) {
            var event;

            if (typeof (Event) === 'function') {
                event = new Event(eventName);
            } else {
                event = document.createEvent('Event'); 
                event.initEvent(eventName, true, true);
            }

            return event;
        }

        // We won't process requests made from any status page
        if (window.location.pathname.indexOf('/status/') === -1)
        {
            // enable sso only if the userAgent is not safari
            if (!/^((?!chrome|android).)*safari/i.test(navigator.userAgent)) {
                enableSSO();
            }
        }
    });

</script> <!--EndDonut-->

   <section id="credit" class="section" aria-label="See what you can do with your free credit"> 
    <div class="row column text-center"> 
     <h2>What can I do with my free account?</h2> 
     <p>Here are just a few ideas of all you can do with Azure</p> 
    </div> 
    <div class="row"> 
     <div class="column medium-4 text-center end"> 
      <div class="row column"> <span class=""> <img src="//azurecomcdn.azureedge.net/cvt-526390d16d87de1877250c5808f92a928069f41676f250913969acdedd7e9a4a/images/shared/free/gep-pages/free-test-deploy.svg" alt="" role="presentation"> </span> 
      </div> 
      <div class="row column row-size2 sd-equalize"> 
       <h3 class="text-heading4">Create personalized experiences with AI</h3> 
      </div> 
      <div class="row column row-size2">
        Build connected, cross-platform experiencestailored to customer interactions using AI and machine learning. 
      </div> 
     </div> 
     <div class="column medium-4 text-center end"> 
      <div class="row column"> <span class=""> <img src="//azurecomcdn.azureedge.net/cvt-526390d16d87de1877250c5808f92a928069f41676f250913969acdedd7e9a4a/images/shared/free/gep-pages/free-experience.svg" alt="" role="presentation"> </span> 
      </div> 
      <div class="row column row-size2 sd-equalize"> 
       <h3 class="text-heading4">Drive innovation for existing and future apps</h3> 
      </div> 
      <div class="row column row-size2">
        Modernize applications through serverless and containers. Deploy Windows and Linux virtual machines across cloud and hybrid environments. 
      </div> 
     </div> 
     <div class="column medium-4 text-center end"> 
      <div class="row column"> <span class=""> <img src="//azurecomcdn.azureedge.net/cvt-526390d16d87de1877250c5808f92a928069f41676f250913969acdedd7e9a4a/images/shared/free/gep-pages/free-gain-insights.svg" alt="" role="presentation"> </span> 
      </div> 
      <div class="row column row-size2 sd-equalize"> 
       <h3 class="text-heading4">Build scalable apps and release features faster</h3>

   <section class="section section-size3" aria-label="What else do I need to know?"> 
    <div class="row column text-center"> 
     <h2>What else do I need to know?</h2> 
    </div> 
    <div class="row"> 
     <div class="column medium-6"> 
      <div class="card card-size01 card--gray20 sd-equalize" data-set="need-to-know-card"> 
       <p class="text-bold">Do I pay anything to start with the Azure free account?</p> 
       <p>No. Starting is free, plus you get a <span class="price-data " data-amount="{&quot;currencies&quot;:{&quot;USD&quot;:200.0,&quot;ARS&quot;:16750.0,&quot;AUD&quot;:280.0,&quot;BRL&quot;:980.0,&quot;CAD&quot;:260.0,&quot;CHF&quot;:200.0,&quot;DKK&quot;:1300.0,&quot;EUR&quot;:170.0,&quot;GBP&quot;:150.0,&quot;HKD&quot;:1600.0,&quot;IDR&quot;:3130000.0,&quot;INR&quot;:14500.0,&quot;JPY&quot;:22500.0,&quot;KRW&quot;:224930.0,&quot;MXN&quot;:4300.0,&quot;MYR&quot;:850.0,&quot;NOK&quot;:1800.0,&quot;NZD&quot;:310.0,&quot;RUB&quot;:12500.0,&quot;SAR&quot;:750.0,&quot;SEK&quot;:1750.0,&quot;TRY&quot;:1440.0,&quot;TWD&quot;:6100.0,&quot;ZAR&quot;:3700.0}}" data-decimals="3"><span class="price-value">$200</span></span> credit you can spend during the first 30 days.</p> 
      </div> 
     </div> 
     <div class="column medium-6"> 
      <div class="card card-size01 card--gray20 sd-equalize" data-set="need-to-know-card"> 
       <p class="text-bold">What happens once I use my <span class="price-data " data-amount="{&quot;currencies&quot;:{&quot;USD&quot;:200.0,&quot;ARS&quot;:16750.0,&quot;AUD&quot;:280.0,&quot;BRL&quot;:980.0,&quot;CAD&quot;:260.0,&quot;CHF&quot;:200.0,&quot;DKK&quot;:1300.0,&quot;EUR&quot;:170.0,&quot;GBP&quot;:150.0,&quot;HKD&quot;:1600.0,&quot;IDR&quot;:3130000.0,&quot;INR&quot;:14500.0,&quot;JPY&quot;:22500.0,&quot;KRW&quot;:224930.0,&quot;MXN&quot;:4300.0,&quot;MYR&quot;:850.0,&quot;NOK&quot;:1800.0,&quot;NZD&quot;:310.0,&quot;RUB&quot;:12500.0,&quot;SAR&quot;:750.0,&quot;SEK&quot;:1750.0,&quot;TRY&quot;:1440.0,&quot;TWD&quot;:6100.0,&quot;ZAR&quot;:3700.0}}" data-decimals="3"><span class="price-value">$200</span></span> free credit or Im at the end of 30 days?</p> 
       <p>Well notify you so you can decide if you want to upgrade to pay-as-you-go pricing and remove the spending limit. If you do, youll have access to free products.* If you dont, your account and products will be disabled, and you'll need to upgrade to resume usage.<br> <span class="text-body5">* Based on resource and region availability.</span></p> 
      </div> 
     </div> 
    </div> 
    <div class="row row-size2"> 
     <div class="column medium-6"> 
      <div class="card card-size01 card--gray20 sd-equalize" data-set="need-to-know-card"> 
       <p class="text-bold">What happens at the end of the 12 months of free products?</p> 
       <p>For 12 months after you upgrade your account, <a href="/en-us/free/free-account-faq/#free-products-table" data-event="area-free-freeaccountfaq-clicked-link">certain amounts</a> of a number of products are free.* After 12 months, youll be billed at the standard pay-as-you-go rates.<br> <span class="text-body5">* Based on resource and region availability.</span></p> 
      </div> 
     </div> 
     <div class="column medium-6"> 
      <div class="card card-size01 card--gray20 sd-equalize" data-set="need-to-know-card"> 
       <p class="text-bold">What do I need to sign up for a free account?</p> 
       <p>All you need is a phone number, a credit card, and a GitHub account or Microsoft account username (formerly Windows Live ID).</p> 
      </div> 
     </div> 
    </div>

    </div>
